There is always a lot to do. But only 1 moment at a time. Only one thing can be done at once. ^ref-40185d05-1-0
To let myself be pulled all over, that is unnessisary.
When there is much to do, the first thing we have to do is prioritize it.<!-- GENERATED-SECTIONS:DO-NOT-EDIT-BELOW -->
